Whereas, everytime I wore MI, I felt that I wasn't really wearing anything. I don't know what this used to smell like when it first launched, but today it's a metallic smelling mess that comes and goes within a few hours. It's crazy how a clone can smell more like the fragrance is supposed to than the original, but that's what happened here. Bottom line, I sold it off pretty cheap and will be getting another bottle of Milestone.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="2276492"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=2276492#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276193" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Sprayed my 2014 bottle 3 hours before the tester.  I went to smell my wrist 20 minutes after applying, the older batch was still considerably stronger than the modern one I had just put on.<br />
<br />
For the old batch smell wise each individual note really pops out during the dry down process. A fresh fruity opening followed by a salty breeze with a marine base.<br />
<br />
The modern batch started with a poorly blended mix of fruit with a strange musty smelling note.  Hardly any marine notes and couldn’t pick up any of the salt notes I did on the vintage.<br />
<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2232686" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Gt63"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2190693"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2190693.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Gt63" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2232686ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2232686" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2190693">Gt63</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-29">07/29/24 08:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Since 1995 even early 2000s this fragrance always was light. It’s designed and also marketed on the creed website as “light notes” it’s nothing wrong with the longevity the issue is you people see a gold bottle thinking it’s a warm amber fragrance. It’s not it’s a light aquatic fragrance that designed to be luxurious and elegant which it is. The scent profile is 9.5/10 easy. Project 2-3hrs mid 4-6hrs. the skin scent you will smell a ambergris/sea mineral on skin for 8-12+hrs till you take a shower. even then you still smell ambergris/sea mineral. <br />
<br />
This was made by Pierre Bourdon who used Green Irish tweed as the foundation of Millésime Impérial and silver mountain water. Green Irish tweed green ozonic, Millésime Impérial light aquatic, silver mountain water the hybrid ozonic/aquatic. Green Irish Tweed being the most powerful. Silver Mountain Water being the medium and Millésime Impérial being the light.<br />
<br />
<br />
The opening bergamot and the Aventus black currant the violet gives it a ozonic transition into the salty aquatic mid. The base is ambergris with white musk. It’s one of the best smelling fragrance I ever smelled and it’s 30+ years old.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is James Bond in his Aston Martin. Bruce Wayne in his Lamborghini. Christian Grey In an Audi R8.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="2232686"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=2232686#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2228300" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:5,&quot;sillage&quot;:4,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; From one of the greatest perfumers ever Pierre Bourdon. Like all light blues designed for people who don’t want overwhelming strong fragrance.<br />
<br />
If you like super synthetics that last 48hrs nuclear this isn’t for you. it’s a light photo realistic smelling fragrance. It is one of the best scent profile ever I could smell it all day. Definitely blind but worthy. I’m not the type person that care for fragrances lasting 8hrs most cheap fragrances last all day. My Batch code F002402 last a good 5-6hrs then goes to a realistic mineral skin scent. I will forever keep this in my creed rotation.<br />
<br />
Something that’s not listed in the notes is ambergris. This dry down very much like Green Irish Tweed you will get the salty mineral ambergris notes on your skin. It’s very addictive. I also realized the Indian sandalwood gives an oceanic wood note as well same as green Irish tweed. When spraying this because it was designed with lighter notes spray it 3 inches from skin. Very close it’s ok if some running occurs. This gets better performance. Creed actually promotes it as a light fragrance so it’s really for people who love lighter fragrances.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="2215509"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=2215509#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2213441" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Fruity opening with a salty note, melon mixed with citruses. Then turns into a fruity musk, which is probably my favorite part. The musk just smells very addictive and sweet. Very bright and is honestly perfect for the summertime. Sadly the performance is not great for the price you pay. Very airy from the beginning, but the first hour of projection is actually quite solid. After this it quickly turns into a close skin scent, and after like 3-5 hours it is almost completely gone. I understand why the opening is so short, but i just wish the dry down lasted a little bit longer and projected better since i enjoy it so much. <br />
<br />
I also feel like the performance is very inconsistent (this seems to be a common Creed thing, since my SMW is the same way), because it some times disappears after 30 minutes while at other times lasting longer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1020219">Apocalypse6vs8</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-01">07/01/24 07:00</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I was fortunate enough to pick up a 2014 batch in the 120ml. size back in 2019. It was being killed back then because of its performance, lack there of to be precise. I got it for under $140US as retailers &amp; discounters were trying to dump it as fast as they could thinking it would keep plummeting because of the bad reviews and negative commentary Millesime Imperial was getting and still does to this day.  Great scent that to me was average on performance in overall projection &amp; longevity. Fast forward to June 2024 and I’ve used it sparingly in the years since while additionally it has gotten better in staying on my skin. Just a beautiful citrus, musk and light marine accord that blends in seamlessly with a soft woods and tat Creed dna that to me has a touch of ambergris in the composition. It still does not project but, the longevity is much better as I get soft and smooth wafts of it nearly 10 hours later from first spaying in the morning before work. It’s like a vacation in a bottle that exudes casual class, elegance and an unassuming sophistication. The scents notes &amp; accords mix to near perfection on my skin giving a light musky skin sweetness that very few fragrances in my collection can match. <br />
<br />
I can’t say with certainty if newer releases have gotten worse or better as I have not tried any other newer batches/formulations of this fragrance. I got lucky with my catch and I can only say that for me, this is as good as any scent that Creed has ever created. The scent is quiet and low key but, it is persistent in staying on the skin and offers the perfect unobtrusive scent bubble that is personal yet, those that are close enough (definitely within arms length) will want to get even closer just to catch a slight whiff of this gorgeous aroma.<br />
<br />
Maceración might help but, I can’t say with certainty that it will.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="2204658"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=2204658#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2204465" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

<br />
Sadly I would probably recommend the clone of this, even though I haven’t tried that one. There’s no point in spending hundreds to only get 100 minutes; kind of defeats the purpose of wearing a fragrance.   <br />
Creed really needs to get the performance thing in order, it’s a bit of a gong show. <br />
This and Green Irish Tweed truly only last two hours on me and then gone. And the average wear time for their fragrances are about 5-6 hours.<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1447620">SmellSharpe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-28">05/28/24 13:51</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Review based on a new 50ml “F batch” bottle.<br />
<br />
Another excellent warm weather Creed fragrance and I continue to be impressed by the recent Creed F batch bottlings.<br />
<br />
This has is a beautiful acquatic/citrus opening with a touch of melon. I strangely get a touch of petroleum/gasoline on the drydown but not enough to be off putting in any way. There is also a very light touch of iris and the drydown is woody/musky but the citrus sticks around. I don’t get sea salt specifically, but it does remind me of the sea.<br />
<br />
Medium projection and quite long lasting for an aquatic/citrus fragrance. More than acceptable in any case. Warm weather wear only for me.<br />
<br />
This is NOT the worth retail price though. Even $250USD/100ml thru the discounters is a bit steep IMO. I am happy with my purchase but I highly recommend testing before buying as Imperial is a little different/funky. Not as safe a blind buy as other Creeds such as Aventus, VIW, Himalaya, GIT, etc.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="2170559"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=2170559#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2166286" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; For some reason my nose is finally picking up those ripe fruit notes where it didn't before and I'm liking it much more. I have also changed where I apply it on my body. padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2096898">FragrancePlease</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-04-24">04/24/24 15:30</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>To give a good review, I bought new from amazon from the creed store. Of all places I know... And when it came i was super exited as this was my first creed fragrance (Owned). And come to my surprise it lasts a good 4-5 hours on my skin with very little loss in Sillage and a moderate projection with an intimate projection in the last hour or so. Absolute lady killer too. Smelt the dupes or so called clones and none have come close enough to where i wouldn't spend the money for the real deal. 10/10 Scent profile really beautiful. New batch too. One of the best mass appealing summer fragrances on the market. Either i got lucky or people went to fragrance stores and under sprayed to see minimal performance. <br />
 I STRONGLY smell this fragrance on my skin or around me for 3-4 hours please test this on your skin but this stuff does not disappoint in performance, or at least id did not for me. I dont know why so many people shit on its longevity when its been nothing but consistant 5 hours with only 5-6 sprays In hot weather too! <br />
<br />
Strong Points:<br />
1. Compliment Monster <br />
2. Extreme appeal to the opposite sex, combining a feminine smoothness with a masculine bold scent, similar to Silver mountain water but IMO a little smoother and more opposite sex appealing.<br />
3. A wonderful and unique scent profile.<br />
4. With a little bit of aquatic soapiness, not an overwhelming amount mind you, smells unbelievably fresh and clean.<br />
5. The longer the fragrance stays on your skin the more woody it becomes and really opens up to an incredibly complex smelling scent (If it lasts)<br />
<br />
Weak Points:<br />
1. Possible poor longevity for some skin types<br />
2. If the projection was just a little bit stronger, and the longevity a little bit longer, this would be the perfect fragrance.<br />
3. Can if you really try to find the smell, smell slightly similar to body wash and a little soapy, for some people not their type.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; There’s definitely way cheaper fragrances that smell similar, that being said, this smells of higher quality, and much smoother than anything that smells similar. It’s a salty, melony aquatic fragrance. Very appropriate for the office, in fact so appropriate it reminds me of the office. If you want the pinnacle of the “blue” fragrances it’s worth a buy, but if you’re expecting some crazy unique smell, you’ll be disappointed. The dry down is more unique, but virtually unsmellable unless someone has their nose to your skin.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="2115074"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=2115074#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2115056" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.85);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Although some on here may say that its performance is not the strongest, I believe that its beauty and uniqueness more than make up for it. I think it’s one of the classiest, most positive fragrances I have ever encountered.<br />
<br />
Its blend of fruity citrus and airy notes creates a scent that is both refreshing yet somehow sophisticated, evoking a sense of positivity and confidence. <br />
<br />
And even though it may not last as long as some other fragrances, its amazing smell makes it worth reapplying throughout the day. <br />
<br />
It’s like summer in a bottle.  It's the perfect scent for those who want to capture the essence of a carefree, sunny day, no matter what the weather is like outside.<br />
<br />
10/10. Please sample as it’s expensive.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="2013539"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=2013539#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2012788" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Creed fragrances are sophisticated classic scents that are not meant to smack you in the face like say Amouage interlude. What creed do best is blend quality materials together to give you a sense of class and elegance without shouting at everyone look I'm here smell me. I really don't think everyone understands what these fragrances by creed represent or what they are designed to do. If you continue to measure certain fragrances against other fragrance houses then yes of course you will be conflicted. But understanding what each house is trying to achieve is they key to appreciating what goes into creating a particular fragrance and what that house is all about. For me creed do it best and they have a fragrance for every season not only that but each of their fragrances can be worn all year round I find most of them can work in all seasons. Fragrance is art and it's subjective if you are willing to pay the price for something that has the best ingredients then I say creed is worth it. padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1949842" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="AUyliong"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1859277"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1859277.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="AUyliong" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1949842ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x0"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1949842" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.86); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1859277">AUyliong</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-10-12">10/12/23 02:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Not sure what the hype was for Millesime Imperial. Maybe it's just my skin chemistry but it doesn't seem all that special. It's very lithe and ozonic. Not much projection or sillage. Longevity is TBD. <br />
<br />
I smell a hint of some spice as well as a hint of gasoline. Somehow it smells fresh though. In the drydown it smells kind of minty and watery at the same time. Not a beast mode frag. Nothing wowing me over but not a bad thing to smell like.<br />

Update: It's transformed into something that smells like a cross between Lysol and windowasher fluid. A hint of Baygon bug spray too.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1949842"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1949842#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1938406" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1938406" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="M-as-Marin"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1202613"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1202613.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="M-as-Marin" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Tom-Ford/Oud-Wood-1826.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.1826.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Oud Wood"title="Oud Wood"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1938406ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1938406" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.73); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1202613">M-as-Marin</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-27">09/27/23 05:06</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I took my time and didn’t rush to review it quickly. Why? Well, some fragrances can give the wrong impressions at first, especially in the wrong seasons of the year. If I had done such a close-minded thing, this review would have probably been completely different than it is today. After almost 30 years on the market, I expected it to still be super unique (which it is to a certain degree) and not remind me of any other fragrance. But as time went on, I realized that even if it smells kinda close to Silver Mountain Water, Erolfa and slight touches of Green Irish Tweed, I still find it to be a better mix except for Green Irish Tweed, which is my favorite scent from the brand.<br />
<br />
TOP NOTES<br />
What I get from this beautiful opening is a refreshing and uplifting combination of fruits and citruses. Finest lemons, zesty bergamot, and that famous blackcurrant note found in Aventus as well. The violet used here is not your typical note found in scents like Dior’s Fahrenheit; it serves to provide an ozonic impression and adds extra depth to the opening. The opening is brief and pleasant before transitioning into the heart notes, which include the brand’s signature accord.<br />
<br />
HEART NOTES<br />
The best part of this composition is the heavenly heart notes that bring everything together in a wonderful way. The ambergris accord in this fragrance is truly exceptional, and it’s no wonder it’s one of my all-time favorite fragrance notes. For those unfamiliar, real ambergris carries the scent of sea salt and musk with a hint of marine accords. To avoid a one-dimensional transition, the blend ensures that the opening notes linger and play a supporting role. This inviting and fresh shift is hard to dislike, and I have yet to meet someone who wouldn’t enjoy such an experience.<br />
<br />
BASE NOTES<br />
The beachy and oceanic vibes persist into the dry-down, where we encounter a clean muskiness. Despite cedarwood and sandalwood being listed as official base notes, I don’t detect them, and the fragrance never takes on a woody character. The base notes of Imperial are comprised of citruses, salt, marine accord, and a more pronounced powdery musk.<br />
<br />
OVERALL<br />
This is a fantastic perfume suitable for anyone who appreciates natural aquatic fragrances. Despite its moderate performance, this scent truly stands out. The delightful combination of marine, fruity, and musky notes strikes a balance that is perfect for personal enjoyment, while its moderate projection ensures those around you can revel in its charm as well.<br />
<br />
Read the full review at scentgrail.com</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1938406"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1938406#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1924941" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1831126">GAD07</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-08">09/08/23 23:07</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>THE BOTTLE GIVES YOU A HINT OF WHAT YOU ARE GOING TO SMELL!<br />
 YEAH ITS GOLD,  THIS IS ROYALTY , WEALTH AND RICHNESS IN A BOTTLE</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1923344"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1923344#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1922955" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1922955" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="criskywalker17"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1266295"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="criskywalker17" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1922955ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1922955" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.82); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1266295">criskywalker17</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-09-08">09/08/23 11:53</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It is clear that perfumery is a very personal thing... <br />
<br />
For me, Millesime Imperial by Creed is my favorite perfume if we only consider the scent and leave aside other parameters such as duration or trail. I have quite a large niche collection with perfumes that I love, from Creed I have Aventus, Aventus cologne, VIW... And every day I go to the closet to smell this and put it on, even if it's a spray. It has become a very special scent for me. <br />
<br />
I am of the opinion that a perfume has to last, and this one lasts a short time and doesn't become as present as others. In the existential journey that all perfume lovers undertake to find the ideal perfume that smells the best, that projects the most, that gives the most compliments, suddenly you find something like this fragrance, a perfume that even if it is not everything you were looking for makes you feel in a very special way and catches you. And you never want to let go. <br />
<br />
It would be my signature fragrance if it weren't for the price (understandable because the ingredients are of high quality and it's a Creed) and the duration, it hurts to pick up a niche perfume and have to spray it on like there's no tomorrow. I wish it lasted much longer, if it did I would sell much of my collection and buy just this. <br />
<br />
Is it worth spending the price on this? Try it, ask yourself what you are looking for, don't be guided by what people say and decide for yourself. If what you need is to buy a single perfume that has a trail, is heavy and attracts attention for meters far away, this is not it, but if you want a more intimate beauty cologne and you are aware that it does not last long, for me it is worth it, and very much so.  Furthermore, people like this perfume very much on me.<br />
<br />
<br />
By the way, I also have Milestone and if you smell them hand in hand you will notice that they have the same concept but the final path is different. If you like Millesime Imperial it is fine to have it for day to day wear.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1922955"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1922955#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1922466" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.81);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

<br />
Overall, it's quite nice. Got this as a decant from Microperfumes. This is another example of why I don't blind buy expensive scents. As has been said by pretty much every reviewer, Gonzo opening! But like every other freshie out there that I've tried, projects well for an hour or less, then it becomes a skin scent for a few hours, then nothing. You'll definitely have to respray midday. It's not even a skin scent in four hours. But I've had that same experience with most freshies I've tried. Citrus notes in particular always dissipate well before the others. But this fragrance is $270 for the 100ML bottle, so I expect performance that this is not delivering. Moreover, the fragrance lacks any defining character that would make it recognizable, so you may as well spend $30 on a bottle of Montblanc Individuel as 30 minutes after you apply no one will know the difference. So this fragrance is a definite "nope" for me and rated "dislike", not because I don't like the scent, while it lasts, but because it doesn't last, and it's way overpriced to be such a poor performer.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Scent 5/5<br />
Longevity 3/5<br />
Sillage 3.5/5</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1847249"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1847249#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1843368" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc1843368" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="The Wolf"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1263755.gif" class="comments-avatar"alt="The Wolf" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Perris-Monte-Carlo/Oud-Imperial-Extrait-37829.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.37829.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Oud Imperial Extrait"title="Oud Imperial Extrait"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma1843368ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd1843368" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1263755">The Wolf</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-05-28">05/28/23 00:52</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This has been one of my favorite fragrances for many years, but I refused to buy another bottle because the performance for the price, makes me crazy. In the Texas heat, my skin eats each spray in about 45 minutes (I've looked at my watch) and by an an hour and half, it's completely undetectable. I literally spray it on my face sometimes so I can enjoy the smell for as long as possible, although this is generally a bad idea 😄<br />
 <br />
Sean John Unforgivable smells good for a couple minutes, but the drydown is synthetic and terrible. I started using Armaf Milestone which is a great substitute with good performance, but I still missed the original because it's natural and smooth.You WILL need to carry a decant of this stuff because it behaves like an EDC, but it's worth it if you can find a deal.<br />
<br />
Here's the deal, if you can afford to spray heavy and spray often, it really doesn't get any better than Millisme Imperial in the summer heat. And if you can afford to spray often, you will get lots of compliments (even if you're sweating) if that's something that matters to you. I've literally never met a single person that doesn't like how this smells. I bought a big flacon (heavily discounted) and I spray the shit out of it. <br />
<br />
A masterpiece that was inspired by a seaside palace of a Saudi Prince. The bottle is gold, because it is the gold standard of warm weather fragrances, created by the brilliant Pierre Bourdon ⚜️<br />
<br />
Scent 10/10<br />
Performance 1/10<br />
<br />
P. S. Watch out for fakes because they are EVERYWHERE. Don't rely on the Creed atomizer trick to detect counterfeits. The only way to know is to get familiar with the scent, or get a genuine decant and compare it with your new bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1843368"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1843368#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1840047" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
Blind smelling I wouldn't call it a marine scent because it leaves such a soft, floral almost powdery impression on me, but what do I know. <br />
<br />

One behind each ear, two on the chest/throat, one on each wrist. 2-3 hours later I couldn't smell it unless I put my wrist to my nose. A lt of die hard fans of the Creed line will say that you've just gone nose blind to it. Naw, I've never experienced a nose bling fragrance out of all the fragrances I've tried or own. I would say if it were their price was for more than a half gallon of it, then it would okay because then, you could just carry around a 10-20 mil. decant and fresh yourself every 20 minutes. That might get you through the day, maybe.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1796315"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1796315#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1796092" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
This fragrance is a masterpiece. Pierre Bourdon is truly a genius.<br />
<br />

<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1408251">Yalcin05</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2023-01-29">01/29/23 16:24</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Unfortunately a lot of people complain about the longevity and Sillage, which I truly can understand since I had the same problem. But Creed had this problem always and it’s nothing new with newer batches or so. Yes the older batches where bit thicker and the ambergris was much stronger and natural, but the newer batches do smell better IMO. I have smelled this stuff since 2009 and I can say it has transformed for sure, but not certainly in a bad way. <br />
<br />
There is no melon anymore I agree specially when I smell my older batches I can see this as a bad thing, but the newer batches have that sweet lemony vibe to it which makes it far more approachable and more a signature scent then before. The saltiness is there but soft smooth, where the older batches could give you headache if ir performed well on your skin during the summer. Therefore I would like to mention that creeds contain 60% naturals as Some houses like Roja even 80%. You have people who adores their longevity and some hates them.. the thing with naturals is.. your skin. You need to have less fat on your body, not to dry skin, not to light skin, and specially your body chemistry should be sour so your PH degree in your body plays a big roll, and your nose ofcourse, how trained and strong is your nose?<br />
<br />
These question will give you the right answers to judge these natural perfumes better. Although creeds are overpriced I can agree, but the scents are definitely great and not generic at all!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="1746897"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=1746897#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1743882" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
The citrus notes now have become a background scent but moved with the salty accords make this such a fresh , sheer scent .<br />
<br />
But what makes this stand out is the musk/oak moss base notes . These notes come in straightaway when the citrus notes dissipates . A few reviewers mentioned leather notes or ambergris , I get oak moss and neither are even listed . <br />
<br />
Whatever it is , it saves this fragrance . It’s actually my first fragrance from the Creed perfume house that I don’t mind . <br />
<br />
Creed to me is way overpriced for such mainstream and sheer scents . I’m not one to skimp on buying niche perfumes , infact I believe quality ingredients are worth every penny.  But with Creed , I usually get too synthetic notes especially in the floral range ( my preferred fragrance group) . <br />
<br />
I believe this is a masculine scent for me and I’ll run it pass my husband but I know he wouldn’t buy a bottle because of the price .</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1291982">Maximus8321</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-29">12/29/22 20:54</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is my #1 perfume from all of my huge collection! My wife asked me which one would I choose if I could only have one and I said Millesime imperial without hesitation! This masterpiece was definitely created way ahead of its time. It is 27 years later now and there is nothing that smells like that on the market. It is so unique and the quality of the ingredients is the finest. I know people compare it to Armaf Milestone, but there is nothing in common between the two except for the shared DNA. I have two bottles of MI and a bottle of Milestone which I got based on the hype around this clone and, to be quite honest, I can't even wear the Milestone as it is a synthetic mess compared to the MI. In my opinion, it comes down to affordability. Some people can afford it and get the MI while others who cannot try to find clones and justify why they chose this over that. The two bottles that I have are from 2020 and 2021 and they both perform above average on my skin. I get about 7-8 hours of longevity with moderate projection and, honestly, it's more than enough for me as I don't mind to reapply this gem throughout the day as I enjoy it so much! I use it year round and I have no issues with performance even in the harshest of cold. Thus, a piece of advice for those who try to decide between getting the MI or one of the clones - GET THE ORIGINAL IF YOU CAN AFFORD IT AND THANK ME LATER:))) This fragrance is truly one of a kind and I don't think anyone will be able to replicate it ever:))))</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1412609">tecfield</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2022-12-21">12/21/22 06:01</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>My review is based on my 2012 bottle. It is an interesting composition of notes. Yes you get the ocean vibe and yes the salt too which are really interesting. If I sniff it deeply I feel salty in my mouth somehow :P<br />
It's citrussy, fruity, aromatic, musky with a hint of woodsy notes. In this version that I have, iris is very prominent. It's not lipsticky like Dior Homme line. If I want to put it in words, it is like you are sitting in front of the ocean in a spring morning when it is not too sunny or hot and the breeze from the ocean is picking some iris scent from a garden nearby ant get to you passing over your fruit salad and some fresh cut citruses. And the table that all these are on is wooden.<br />
Based on this composition of notes, longevity is not and cannot be good -- it is just a sad fact.<br />
To my nose, this is very unisex and ladies can pull it off easily even younger ladies.<br />
For me, this is something that I enjoy spraying it on a tester strip and leave it at my desk so I can get a whiff now and then but not probably something I would like to wear. I think there are better summer/spring choices in my collection. Enough to have purchased a full bottle to wear myself, in summer.<br />
<br />
I do agree that the silage is poor, but I can smell it on myself for long enough to feel happy, and that's all that really matters … since I live on a farm with a bunch of animals and a husband with very compromised olfactory abilities.<br />
<br />
A review I read on LuckyScent described this as a "positive" fragrance, and I think that is how it really works for me.<br />
<br />
Citrus and marine.  Nothing dark and potentially disturbing here at all.  Clear skies, vast blue horizon, looking forward to the new day and a good future.  Fresh and subtly stimulating, with still a way of being soft.  <br />
<br />

NOT SAYING THAT IT'S ANYTHING TERRIBLE, JUST OVERHYPED AND OVERPRICED.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="466"comment_id="595517"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Creed/Millesime-Imperial-466.html?ccid=595517#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1121414" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.78);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
